     1	import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * User information type (without password)
     5	 */
     6	export type UserInfo = {
     7	  id: string;
     8	  uid: string;
     9	  email: string | null;
    10	  phone: string | null;
    11	  name: string;
    12	  role: 'USER' | 'ADMIN';
    13	  isVerified: boolean;
    14	  shippingAddress: string | null;
    15	  postalCode: string | null;
    16	  createdAt: Date;
    17	  updatedAt: Date;
    18	};
    19	
    20	/**
    21	 * Generic user query function
    22	 * Reduces duplication in getUserById, getUserByEmail, getUserByPhone
    23	 */
    24	export async function queryUser(where: {
    25	  id?: string;
    26	  email?: string;
    27	  phone?: string;
    28	}): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
    29	  const supabase = createClient();
    30	
    31	  let query = supabase
    32	    .from('users')
    33	    .select(
    34	      'id, uid, email, phone, name, role, isVerified, shippingAddress, postalCode, createdAt, updatedAt'
    35	    )
    36	    .limit(1);
    37	
    38	  if (where.id) {
    39	    query = query.eq('id', where.id);
    40	  } else if (where.email) {
    41	    query = query.eq('email', where.email);
    42	  } else if (where.phone) {
    43	    query = query.eq('phone', where.phone);
    44	  } else {
    45	    return null;
    46	  }
    47	
    48	  const { data, error } = await query.single();
    49	
    50	  if (error || !data) {
    51	    return null;
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  // Convert string dates to Date objects for type compatibility
    55	  return {
    56	    ...data,
    57	    createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
    58	    updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
    59	  };
    60	}
    61	
    62	/**
    63	 * Check if a user exists with the given identifier
    64	 * Used for uniqueness validation
    65	 */
    66	export async function checkUserExists(
    67	  identifier: { email?: string; phone?: string },
    68	  excludeUserId?: string
    69	): Promise<boolean> {
    70	  const supabase = createClient();
    71	
    72	  // Build OR conditions
    73	  const conditions = [];
    74	
    75	  if (identifier.email) {
    76	    conditions.push(`email.eq.${identifier.email}`);
    77	  }
    78	
    79	  if (identifier.phone) {
    80	    conditions.push(`phone.eq.${identifier.phone}`);
    81	  }
    82	
    83	  if (conditions.length === 0) {
    84	    return false;
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  let query = supabase
    88	    .from('users')
    89	    .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
    90	    .or(conditions.join(','));
    91	
    92	  if (excludeUserId) {
    93	    query = query.neq('id', excludeUserId);
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  const { count, error } = await query;
    97	
    98	  if (error) {
    99	    return false;
   100	  }
   101	
   102	  return (count ?? 0) > 0;
   103	}

  1096	export async function createProduct(data: {
  1097	  name: string;
  1098	  description: string;
  1099	  price: number;
  1100	  discountPercent?: number | null;
  1101	  stock: number;
  1102	  images?: string[];

  1104	  tagIds?: string[];
  1105	  hasVariants?: boolean;
  1106	  isFeatured?: boolean;
  1107	  isActive?: boolean;
  1108	}): Promise<ProductWithRelations> {
  1109	  log.info('Creating product', {
  1110	    name: data.name,
  1111	    price: data.price,
  1112	    stock: data.stock,
  1113	  });
  1114	
  1115	  try {
  1116	    // Validate required fields
  1117	    if (!data.name || !data.description) {
  1118	      log.warn('Missing required product fields', { name: data.name });
  1119	      throw new Error('Product name and description are required');
  1120	    }
  1121

  1123	      log.warn('Invalid product price', { price: data.price });

  1125	    }
  1126	
  1127	    if (data.stock < 0) {
  1128	      log.warn('Invalid product stock', { stock: data.stock });
  1129	      throw new Error('Stock cannot be negative');
  1130	    }
  1131	
  1132	    const supabase = createClient();
  1133	
  1134	    // Generate UUID for the product
  1135	    const productId = randomUUID();
  1136	
  1137	    // Create product
  1138	    const { data: product, error } = await supabase
  1139	      .from('products')
  1140	      .insert({
  1141	        id: productId,
  1142	        name: data.name,
  1143	        description: data.description,
  1144	        price: data.price,
  1145	        discountPercent: data.discountPercent || null,
  1146	        stock: data.stock,
  1147	        images: data.images || [],
  1148	        categoryId: data.categoryId || null,
  1149	        hasVariants: data.hasVariants !== undefined ? data.hasVariants : false,
  1150	        isFeatured: data.isFeatured !== undefined ? data.isFeatured : false,
  1151	        isActive: data.isActive !== undefined ? data.isActive : true,
  1152	        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  1153	      })
  1154	      .select()
  1155	      .single();
  1156	
  1157	    if (error || !product) {
  1158	      log.error('Failed to create product', { error });
  1159	      throw new Error('Unable to create product');
  1160	    }

     1	# Getting Supabase API Keys For Tests
     2	
     3	Use a disposable local or hosted Supabase project for integration and E2E tests.
     4	Never run tests against a customer or live database that contains real user
     5	data.
     6	
     7	## Local Supabase
     8	
     9	```bash
    10	npx supabase start
    11	npx supabase db reset
    12	```
    13	
    14	The CLI prints a local API URL and keys. Put them in `tests/.env`:
    15	
    16	```bash
    17	NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=http://127.0.0.1:54321
    18	NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=<local-publishable-or-anon-key>
    19	SUPABASE_SECRET_KEY=<local-secret-or-service-role-key>
    20	```
    21	
    22	Local Supabase service-role JWTs are accepted only for local URLs. Hosted test
    23	projects must use a Supabase secret key.
    24	
    25	## Hosted Supabase
    26	
    27	1. Create a dedicated test project in the Supabase dashboard.
    28	2. Apply the schema from this repository with `npx supabase db push`.
    29	3. Open **Project Settings** -> **API**.
    30	4. Copy the project URL, publishable key, and secret key into `tests/.env`.
    31	
    32	## Safety Notes
    33	
    34	- `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` can be used by browser code.
    35	- `SUPABASE_SECRET_KEY` is server/test-only and bypasses RLS.
    36	- Do not commit `.env`, `tests/.env`, secret keys, or service-role JWTs.
    37	- Integration tests refuse remote Supabase URLs unless
    38	  `TEST_ALLOW_DESTRUCTIVE_DB=I_UNDERSTAND_TEST_DATABASE_IS_DESTRUCTIVE` is set
    39	  for a dedicated disposable hosted test project.
    40	- Integration tests refuse configured Redis credentials unless
    41	  `TEST_ALLOW_SHARED_REDIS=I_UNDERSTAND_TEST_REDIS_IS_DESTRUCTIVE` is set for a
    42	  dedicated disposable Redis instance.
    43	- E2E database helpers refuse remote Supabase URLs by default because they
    44	  delete and insert rows. Use local Supabase for normal development, or set
    45	  `E2E_ALLOW_DESTRUCTIVE_DB=I_UNDERSTAND_E2E_DATABASE_IS_DESTRUCTIVE` only for
    46	  a dedicated disposable hosted test project.
    47	- Use `E2E_BLOCKED_SUPABASE_REFS=ref_one,ref_two` to block known non-test
    48	  project refs in E2E runs.
    49	- If your boilerplate setup does not persist OTPs, configure
    50	  `E2E_STATIC_OTP_CODE` to the deterministic code accepted by the test app
    51	  before running OTP journeys.
    52	
    53	## Verify Keys
    54	
    55	```bash
    56	npx tsx tests/verify-supabase-keys.ts
    57	```
    58	
    59	Expected result: the publishable-key check can read public catalog data, and the
    60	secret-key check can write and clean up test rows.

    35	export async function validateEmailUniqueness(
    36	  email: string | undefined,
    37	  excludeUserId?: string
    38	): Promise<void> {
    39	  if (email === undefined) return;
    40	
    41	  // Validate format

    43	    log.warn('Invalid email format', { email });
    44	    throw new Error('Invalid email format.');
    45	  }

    47	  // Check uniqueness
    48	  if (email) {
    49	    const exists = await checkUserExists({ email }, excludeUserId);
    50	    if (exists) {
    51	      log.warn('Email already in use', { email });
    52	      throw new Error('This email is already in use.');
    53	    }
    54	  }
    55	}

    62	  phone: string | undefined,
    63	  excludeUserId?: string
    64	): Promise<void> {
    65	  if (phone === undefined) return;
    66

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	import {
     2	  parsePhoneNumberFromString,
     3	  type CountryCode,
     4	} from 'libphonenumber-js';
     5	
     6	const easternArabicDigitStart = 0x06f0;
     7	const arabicIndicDigitStart = 0x0660;
     8	
     9	export function normalizeDigits(text: string): string {
    10	  if (!text) return text;
    11	
    12	  return Array.from(text)
    13	    .map((char) => {
    14	      const code = char.charCodeAt(0);
    15	      if (
    16	        code >= easternArabicDigitStart &&
    17	        code <= easternArabicDigitStart + 9
    18	      ) {
    19	        return String(code - easternArabicDigitStart);
    20	      }
    21	      if (code >= arabicIndicDigitStart && code <= arabicIndicDigitStart + 9) {
    22	        return String(code - arabicIndicDigitStart);
    23	      }
    24	      return char;
    25	    })
    26	    .join('');
    27	}
    28	
    29	export function containsRightToLeftCharacters(text: string): boolean {
    30	  if (!text) return false;
    31	
    32	  return /[\u0590-\u08FF\uFB1D-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF]/.test(text);
    33	}
    34	
    35	export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
    36	  const trimmed = name.trim();
    37	  if (!trimmed) return false;
    38	  if (trimmed.length > 120) return false;
    39	
    40	  return /^[\p{L}\p{M}][\p{L}\p{M}\s.'-]*$/u.test(trimmed);
    41	}
    42	
    43	export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
    44	  if (!phone) return phone;
    45	
    46	  const defaultCountry = (
    47	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
    48	  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
    49	  let normalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
    50	
    51	  normalized = normalized.replace(/(?!^)\+/g, '');
    52	  if (normalized.startsWith('00')) {
    53	    normalized = `+${normalized.slice(2)}`;
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  try {
    57	    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
    58	    if (parsed?.isValid()) {
    59	      return parsed.number;
    60	    }
    61	  } catch {
    62	    return normalized;
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  return normalized;
    66	}
    67	
    68	export function isValidPhoneNumber(phone: string): boolean {
    69	  if (!phone) return false;
    70	
    71	  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
    72	  const defaultCountry = (
    73	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
    74	  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
    75	
    76	  try {
    77	    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
    78	    return parsed?.isValid() ?? false;
    79	  } catch {
    80	    return false;
    81	  }
    82	}

  1508	// ========== PRODUCT MEDIA FUNCTIONS ==========
  1509	
  1510	/**
  1511	 * Add media to product
  1512	 */
  1513	export async function addProductMedia(data: {
  1514	  productId: string;
  1515	  variantId?: string;
  1516	  type: MediaType;
  1517	  url: string;
  1518	  alt?: string;
  1519	  order?: number;
  1520	  isDefault?: boolean;
  1521	}): Promise<ProductMedia> {
  1522	  const supabase = createClient();
  1523	
  1524	  // Check if there are any existing media for this product/variant
  1525	  let query = supabase
  1526	    .from('product_media')
  1527	    .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true })
  1528	    .eq('productId', data.productId);
  1529	
  1530	  if (data.variantId) {
  1531	    query = query.eq('variantId', data.variantId);
  1532	  } else {
  1533	    query = query.is('variantId', null);
  1534	  }
  1535	
  1536	  const { count: existingMediaCount } = await query;
  1537	
  1538	  // If this is the first media, make it default automatically (unless explicitly set to false)
  1539	  const shouldBeDefault = data.isDefault ?? existingMediaCount === 0;
  1540	
  1541	  // If this is set as default, unset any existing default for the same product/variant
  1542	  if (shouldBeDefault) {
  1543	    let updateQuery = supabase
  1544	      .from('product_media')
  1545	      .update({ isDefault: false })
  1546	      .eq('productId', data.productId)
  1547	      .eq('isDefault', true);
  1548	
  1549	    if (data.variantId) {
  1550	      updateQuery = updateQuery.eq('variantId', data.variantId);
  1551	    } else {
  1552	      updateQuery = updateQuery.is('variantId', null);
  1553	    }
  1554	
  1555	    await updateQuery;
  1556	  }
  1557	
  1558	  // Create media
  1559	  const mediaId = randomUUID();
  1560	  const { data: media, error } = await supabase
  1561	    .from('product_media')
  1562	    .insert({
  1563	      id: mediaId,
  1564	      productId: data.productId,
  1565	      variantId: data.variantId || null,
  1566	      type: data.type,
  1567	      url: data.url,
  1568	      alt: data.alt || null,
  1569	      order: data.order ?? 0,
  1570	      isDefault: shouldBeDefault,
  1571	    })
  1572	    .select()
  1573	    .single();
  1574	
  1575	  if (error || !media) {
  1576	    log.error('Failed to add product media', { error });
  1577	    throw new Error('Unable to add product media');
  1578	  }
  1579	
  1580	  return media;
  1581	}

    10	async function postHandler(req: NextRequest) {
    11	  // Extract client info for activity logging
    12	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    13	
    14	  try {
    15	    const body = await req.json();
    16	    const { identifier, email, phone, password, name } = body;
    17	    const providedIdentifier = identifier || email || phone;
    18	
    19	    // Validate required fields (name is optional)
    20	    if (!providedIdentifier || !password) {
    21	      return NextResponse.json(
    22	        { error: 'Email or phone number and password are required.' },
    23	        { status: 400 }
    24	      );
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    const normalizedIdentifier = String(providedIdentifier).trim();
    28	    const identifierType = detectIdentifierType(normalizedIdentifier);
    29	
    30	    if (identifierType === 'invalid') {
    31	      return NextResponse.json(
    32	        { error: 'Enter a valid email address or phone number.' },
    33	        { status: 400 }
    34	      );
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    // Create user (validation happens in service)
    38	    // If name is not provided, use empty string as default
    39	    const user = await createUser({
    40	      email: identifierType === 'email' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    41	      phone: identifierType === 'phone' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    42	      password,
    43	      name: name || '',
    44	    });
    45	
    46	    // Log successful registration (fire-and-forget)
    47	    logUserActivity({
    48	      userId: user.id,
    49	      activityType: 'REGISTER',
    50	      ipAddress,
    51	      userAgent,
    52	      success: true,
    53	      metadata: {
    54	        identifier_type: identifierType,
    55	      },
    56	    }).catch((err) => {
    57	      log.warn('Failed to log registration', {
    58	        userId: user.id,
    59	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    60	      });
    61	    });
    62	
    63	    return NextResponse.json(
    64	      {
    65	        success: true,
    66	        message: 'Account created successfully.',
    67	        user: {
    68	          id: user.id,
    69	          email: user.email,
    70	          name: user.name,
    71	          role: user.role,
    72	        },
    73	      },
    74	      { status: 201 }
    75	    );
    76	  } catch (error) {
    77	    console.error('Registration error:', error);
    78	
    79	    // Log failed registration (fire-and-forget)
    80	    logUserActivity({
    81	      activityType: 'REGISTER',
    82	      ipAddress,
    83	      userAgent,
    84	      success: false,
    85	      errorMessage:
    86	        error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Registration failed',
    87	    }).catch((err) => {
    88	      log.warn('Failed to log registration failure', {
    89	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    90	      });
    91	    });
    92	
    93	    // Return user-friendly error message
    94	    return NextResponse.json(
    95	      {
    96	        error:
    97	          error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unable to create account.',
    98	      },
    99	      { status: 400 }
   100	    );
   101	  }
   102	}

    18	export default function RegisterPage() {

    21	    name: '',
    22	    identifier: '', // Can be email or phone
    23	    password: '',

    25	  });
    26	  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
    27	  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    28	  const [successMessage, setSuccessMessage] = useState('');
    29	  const [errorMessage, setErrorMessage] = useState('');
    30	  const [rateLimitRetryAfter, setRateLimitRetryAfter] = useState<number | null>(
    31	    null
    32	  );
    33	
    34	  // Detect if identifier is email or phone
    35	  const detectIdentifierType = (
    36	    value: string
    37	  ): 'email' | 'phone' | 'invalid' => {
    38	    const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
    39	    // Normalize phone number before validation.
    40	    const normalizedPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(value);
    41	
    42	    if (emailRegex.test(value)) return 'email';
    43	    if (isValidPhoneNumber(normalizedPhone)) return 'phone';
    44	    return 'invalid';
    45	  };
    46	
    47	  const validateForm = () => {
    48	    const newErrors: Record<string, string> = {};
    49	
    50	    // Validate name if provided (optional but must be valid if present)
    51	    if (formData.name.trim() && !isValidName(formData.name)) {
    52	      newErrors.name =
    53	        'Name can contain letters, spaces, hyphens, periods, and apostrophes.';
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    if (!formData.identifier.trim()) {
    57	      newErrors.identifier = 'Email or phone number is required.';
    58	    } else {
    59	      const type = detectIdentifierType(formData.identifier);
    60	      if (type === 'invalid') {
    61	        newErrors.identifier = 'Enter a valid email address or phone number.';
    62	      }
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    if (!formData.password) {
    66	      newErrors.password = 'Password is required.';
    67	    } else if (formData.password.length < 8) {
    68	      newErrors.password = 'Password must be at least 8 characters.';
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    if (formData.password !== formData.confirmPassword) {
    72	      newErrors.confirmPassword = 'Passwords do not match.';
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    setErrors(newErrors);
    76	    return Object.keys(newErrors).length === 0;
    77	  };
    78	
    79	  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    80	    e.preventDefault();
    81	    setErrorMessage('');
    82	    setSuccessMessage('');
    83	    setRateLimitRetryAfter(null);
    84	
    85	    if (!validateForm()) {
    86	      return;
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    setIsLoading(true);
    90	
    91	    try {
    92	      const identifierType = detectIdentifierType(formData.identifier);
    93	
    94	      if (identifierType !== 'phone' && identifierType !== 'email') {
    95	        throw new Error('Enter a valid email address or phone number.');
    96	      }
    97	
    98	      const identifier =
    99	        identifierType === 'phone'
   100	          ? normalizePhoneNumber(formData.identifier)
   101	          : formData.identifier;
   102	
   103	      const response = await fetch('/api/auth/register', {
   104	        method: 'POST',
   105	        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   106	        body: JSON.stringify({
   107	          identifier,
   108	          password: formData.password,
   109	          name: formData.name,
   110	        }),
   111	      });
   112	
   113	      if (response.status === 429) {
   114	        const rateLimitData = await response.json();
   115	        setRateLimitRetryAfter(rateLimitData.retryAfter || Date.now() + 120000);
   116	        setIsLoading(false);
   117	        return;
   118	      }
   119	
   120	      const data = await response.json();
   121	      if (!response.ok) {
   122	        throw new Error(data.error || 'Unable to create account.');
   123	      }
   124	
   125	      const signInResult = await signIn('credentials', {
   126	        identifier,
   127	        password: formData.password,
   128	        redirect: false,
   129	      });
   130	
   131	      if (signInResult?.error) {
   132	        setSuccessMessage('Account created. Use the sign-in form to continue.');
   133	        return;
   134	      }
   135	
   136	      if (signInResult?.ok) {
   137	        router.push('/');
   138	        return;
   139	      }

     3	/**
     4	 * Clean up all E2E test data from the database
     5	 * Uses pattern matching to identify test data by prefix
     6	 *
     7	 * IMPORTANT: This only cleans up data created by E2E tests (e2e-* prefix)
     8	 * It will NOT affect real/production data
     9	 */
    10	export async function cleanupE2ETestData(): Promise<void> {
    11	  const supabase = createE2ESupabaseClient();
    12	
    13	  console.log('Cleaning up E2E test data...');
    14	
    15	  // Delete test transaction items first (foreign key constraint)
    16	  const { error: itemsError } = await supabase
    17	    .from('transaction_items')
    18	    .delete()
    19	    .like('productId', 'e2e-product-%');
    20

    23	      `Warning: Could not cleanup transaction items: ${itemsError.message}`
    24	    );
    25	  }

    27	  // Delete test transactions

    29	    .from('transactions')
    30	    .delete()
    31	    .or('transactionCode.like.TX-E2E%,phone.like.%e2e%');
    32

    36

    65	    .like('id', 'e2e-product-%');

    69	  }

    92	    );

    95	  // Delete test users (last, due to foreign key constraints)
    96	  const { error: userError } = await supabase
    97	    .from('users')
    98	    .delete()
    99	    .like('id', 'e2e-user-%');
   100	
   101	  if (userError) {
   102	    console.warn(`Warning: Could not cleanup users: ${userError.message}`);
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  console.log('E2E cleanup complete');
   106	}

   108	/**
   109	 * Clean up test data for a specific product
   110	 */
   111	export async function cleanupProduct(productId: string): Promise<void> {
   112	  if (!productId.startsWith('e2e-product-')) {
   113	    throw new Error(
   114	      `Cannot cleanup non-E2E product: ${productId}. ` +
   115	        'Only products with e2e-product- prefix can be cleaned up.'
   116	    );
   117	  }
   118	
   119	  const supabase = createE2ESupabaseClient();
   120	
   121	  // Delete related transaction items
   122	  await supabase.from('transaction_items').delete().eq('productId', productId);
   123	
   124	  // Delete product media
   125	  await supabase.from('product_media').delete().eq('productId', productId);
   126	
   127	  // Delete product variants
   128	  await supabase.from('product_variants').delete().eq('productId', productId);
   129	
   130	  // Delete the product
   131	  const { error } = await supabase
   132	    .from('products')
   133	    .delete()
   134	    .eq('id', productId);
   135	
   136	  if (error) {
   137	    console.warn(
   138	      `Warning: Could not cleanup product ${productId}: ${error.message}`
   139	    );
   140	  }

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# Supabase RLS Notes
     2	
     3	Supabase projects should enable Row Level Security on tables exposed through the
     4	Data API. This boilerplate enables RLS in
     5	`supabase/migrations/20260531190011_initial_public_schema.sql` and grants
     6	browser roles read-only access only to public catalog data.
     7	
     8	## Checklist
     9	
    10	- Enable RLS on public tables that are reachable through Supabase APIs.
    11	- Grant access to `anon` and `authenticated` roles only when the table is intentionally exposed.
    12	- Keep secret keys and service credentials out of client bundles.
    13	- Prefer `security_invoker = true` for views on Postgres versions that support it.
    14	- Avoid security-definer functions in exposed schemas.
    15	- Test policies with authenticated and anonymous sessions before launch.
    16	
    17	## Default Public Tables
    18	
    19	The initial migration grants `SELECT` policies to `anon` and `authenticated` for
    20	active categories, tags, active products, active variants, product media,
    21	product-tag joins, and site settings. User, transaction, invoice, promo-code
    22	usage, wishlist, and activity-log tables stay server-only by default.
    23	
    24	## Server Access
    25	
    26	Application services use `SUPABASE_SECRET_KEY` from server-only code. That key
    27	must never be exposed through `NEXT_PUBLIC_*` variables, client bundles, browser
    28	logs, screenshots, docs, or checked-in fixtures.
    29	
    30	## Payment Schema Validation
    31	
    32	The built-in payment schema targets Stripe and PayPal:
    33	
    34	```bash
    35	psql "$DATABASE_URL" -v ON_ERROR_STOP=1 -f scripts/db/validate_payment_schema.sql
    36	```
    37	
    38	See `database/schema-contract.md` for the expected payment enum values and transaction columns.

import { defineConfig } from 'vitest/config';
import path from 'path';

/**
 * Integration Tests Configuration - Sequential Execution
 *
 * Integration tests access the real Supabase database and Redis cache.
 * They MUST run sequentially to avoid:
 * - Database state conflicts (tests sharing/modifying the same data)
 * - Race conditions in cleanup utilities
 * - Foreign key constraint violations from concurrent operations
 *
 * Key settings:
 * - pool: 'forks' - Use process forks for better isolation
 * - singleFork: true - All tests run in a single process sequentially
 * - fileParallelism: false - Disable file-level parallelism
 * - sequence.concurrent: false - Disable test-level concurrency
 */
export default defineConfig({
  test: {
    globals: true,
    environment: 'node',
    setupFiles: ['./setup.ts', './integration/setup.ts'],
    include: ['integration/**/*.test.ts'],
    exclude: ['node_modules', 'dist'],
    testTimeout: 60000, // Longer timeout for DB operations
    hookTimeout: 60000, // Longer timeout for cleanup hooks
    teardownTimeout: 30000,
    // Disable file-level parallelism - run files one at a time
    fileParallelism: false,
    // Run integration tests sequentially to avoid database conflicts
    pool: 'forks',
    poolOptions: {
      forks: {
        // Use a single fork to ensure sequential execution
        singleFork: true,
        // No parallel forks
        isolate: true,
      },
    },
    // Ensure tests within files also run sequentially
    sequence: {
      concurrent: false,
    },
    deps: {
      optimizer: {
        ssr: {
          include: ['@upstash/redis'],
        },
      },
    },
  },
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src'),
      '@tests': path.resolve(__dirname, './'),
      '@mocks': path.resolve(__dirname, './mocks'),
      '@fixtures': path.resolve(__dirname, './fixtures'),
      '@utils': path.resolve(__dirname, './utils'),
    },
  },
});
import { defineConfig } from 'vitest/config';
import path from 'path';

/**
 * Unit Tests Configuration - Fully Parallelized
 *
 * Unit tests use mocks (vi.mock) and don't access real databases,
 * so they can safely run in parallel across multiple threads.
 *
 * Key settings:
 * - pool: 'threads' - Use thread-based parallelization (faster than forks)
 * - singleThread: false - Allow multiple threads
 * - isolate: true - Each test file runs in isolation
 * - fileParallelism: true - Run test files in parallel
 */
export default defineConfig({
  test: {
    globals: true,
    environment: 'node',
    setupFiles: ['./setup.ts'],
    include: ['unit/**/*.test.ts'],

    // Enable file-level parallelism

    pool: 'threads',
    poolOptions: {
      threads: {
        // Allow multiple threads for parallel execution
        singleThread: false,
        // Isolate each test file
        isolate: true,
        // Use available CPU cores (default behavior)
        minThreads: 1,
        maxThreads: undefined, // Uses number of CPUs
      },
    },
    coverage: {
      provider: 'v8',
      reporter: ['text', 'json', 'html', 'lcov'],
      exclude: [
        'node_modules/',
        'dist/',
        '**/*.config.ts',
        '**/setup.ts',
        '**/mocks/**',
        '**/fixtures/**',
      ],
    },
    deps: {
      optimizer: {
        ssr: {
          include: ['@upstash/redis'],
        },
      },
    },
  },
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src'),
      '@tests': path.resolve(__dirname, './'),

import 'server-only';
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto';
import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
import { PaginatedResponse, StockVerificationResult } from '@/types/api';
import { log } from '@/lib/logger';
import type { PaymentProvider } from '@/lib/payments/providers';

/**
 * Generate a unique transaction code
 * Format: TX-XXXXXX (e.g., TX-A1B2C3)
 */
export function generateTransactionCode(): string {
  const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789';
  let code = 'TX-';

  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
    code += chars.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length));
  }

  return code;
}

# task005: Supabase Schema And Seed Readiness

Status: Finalized; live DB validation and combined review remain blocked

## Goal

Make the Supabase schema, generated types, migrations, and seed/onboarding story suitable for an open-source boilerplate.

## Start Here

- Read `tasks/open-source-boilerplate-conversion/handoff.md`.
- Read `/home/dexter/.agents/skills/supabase/SKILL.md` because this task touches Supabase.
- Read `/home/dexter/.shared-agent-skills/codex-review-mode/SKILL.md`.

## Files To Inspect First

- `database/schema-contract.md`
- `database/schema-dumps/`
- `migrations/`
- `scripts/db/validate_payment_schema.sql`
- `src/types/supabase.ts`
- `src/lib/supabase/server.ts`
- `src/lib/supabase/middleware.ts`
- `tests/docs/GETTING_SUPABASE_KEYS.md`
- `tests/fixtures/`
- `tests/integration/setup.ts`

## Requirements

- Ensure schema docs describe a fresh boilerplate setup, not preview/production Kitia parity.
- Remove or neutralize schema dump files if they contain private project-specific metadata or are not useful for public setup.
- Keep generated Supabase types aligned with the intended public schema.
- Provide a safe local/setup migration path. Do not invent migration filenames manually; use Supabase CLI conventions if creating new migrations.
- Provide optional seed data or fixture guidance using neutral English products/users and no private CDN URLs.
- Review RLS/security docs for public-template accuracy.
- Do not expose service-role/secret keys in client code or docs.

## Acceptance Criteria

- A new user can understand how to provision Supabase and apply the schema.
- `src/types/supabase.ts` matches current intended schema, including only `STRIPE` and `PAYPAL` payment methods.
- No schema docs refer to private preview/production project refs or private Supabase keys.
- Fixture data uses neutral domains such as `example.com` and local/test image URLs.

## Verification To Run

- `npm run verify`
- `npm run lint`
- `npm run build`
- `psql "$DATABASE_URL" -v ON_ERROR_STOP=1 -f scripts/db/validate_payment_schema.sql` when a configured database is available.
